He was from an extremely poor family and was always on the brink of starvation. At the age of 10, someone gave me a Trigonometry book by Prof Sidney Luxton Loney. I had studied from the same book, while I was in school.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 14pt; line-height: 150%;\">In 1.5 years Ramanujan mastered Loney\u2019s book, and he started churning out his own theorems. He could NOT even afford to buy a ream of paper, as Indians were slaves of the British. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-lbCgIhqENDs/Trefwj4doiI/AAAAAAAAHyY/9RpvYJ_UDa8/s1600/imagesCA7V3043.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-lbCgIhqENDs/Trefwj4doiI/AAAAAAAAHyY/9RpvYJ_UDa8/s1600/imagesCA7V3043.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 14pt; line-height: 150%;\">A couple of well wishers , on noticing his extra-ordinary memory and genius , literally a Syamantaka diamond in the gutter, encouraged him to write to Prof Henry Frederick Baker of Cambridge University, along with some of his original theorems . Baker being in the Algebraic Geometry field ignored this letter. Ramanujan then send the same to Trigonometry expert Prof Ernest William Hobson <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>. He too ignored Ramanujan. Then someone suggested that he must write to Prof GH Hardy . 25 year old Ramanujan wrote to Hardy on 16<sup>th</sup> Jan 1913. The <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Mathematical wonder or</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 14pt; line-height: 150%;\"> </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 14pt; line-height: 150%;\">120 statements of theorems on infinite series, improper integrals, continued fractions, and number theory of theorems in divergent series, did NOT allow Hardy and Mathematical expert John Edensor Littlewood to sleep that night\u2014such was the release of adrenaline, on reading the work of a rare genius..<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 14pt; line-height: 150%;\">Ramanujan wrote : <em><span style=\"color: blue;\">\u201cI beg to introduce myself to you as a clerk in the Accounts Department of the Port Trust Office at Madras on a salary of only <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>\u00a3 20 per annum. I have had no university education but I have undergone the ordinary school course. After leaving school I have been employing the spare time at my disposal to work at mathematics. I have not trodden through the conventional regular course which is followed in a university course, but I am striking out a new path for myself. I have</span><span style=\"color: blue;\"> made a special investigation of divergent series in general and the results I get are termed by the local mathematicians as \u201cstartling\u201c\u2026 I would request you to go through the enclosed papers. Being poor, if you are convinced that there is anything of value I would like to have my theorems published. I have not given the actual investigations nor the expressions that I get but I have indicated the lines on which I proceed. Being inexperienced I would very highly value any advice you give me \u201c.</span></em> <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 14pt; line-height: 150%;\">The letter has become the most important historical document in Mathematics. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>In fact, \u2018this letter is one of the most exciting mathematical letters ever written.</span><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 14pt; line-height: 150%;\"> </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 14pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 14pt; line-height: 150%;\">Hardy went out of his way to pull strings to get Ramanjan to England. Today in hindsight , this was the reason why Ramanujan died at the young age of 32.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 14pt; line-height: 150%;\">Ramanujan's mother resisted at first--high-caste Indians shunned travel to foreign lands--but finally gave in, ostensibly after a vision of the family deity , Goddess Namagiri ( Vishnu avatar half man half lion, Lord Narasimhan\u2019s consort ). . </span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-FNjh1lvVeT4/TriXslh875I/AAAAAAAAH0I/8O3VqyJhNLU/s1600/nam_fort2.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"213\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-FNjh1lvVeT4/TriXslh875I/AAAAAAAAH0I/8O3VqyJhNLU/s320/nam_fort2.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://0.gvt0.com/vi/TZniZ7xKvZA/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/TZniZ7xKvZA&fs=1&source=uds\" />\n<param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" />\n<embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/TZniZ7xKvZA&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: magenta; font-size: large;\">Ramanujan and his mentor Narayana Iyer , a Manager of Madras Port trust&nbsp; sat in the centre of the 4 pillared Mandapam at Namakkal near Chenani,facing Goddess Namagiri ( see picture above)&nbsp;, for three days, listening to stotrams . Suddenly Ramanujan woke up from a deep slumber and told his well wisher that the Goddess has permitted him to go to England&nbsp;. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: magenta; font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">The stotram in the video is written by Adi Sankaracharya in 2000 BC at Kaladi Kerala. He was used to tropical climate and was a strict vegetarian. However, all of his well-wishers prevailed upon him and finally Ramanujan left Madras by S.S. Navesa on March 17, 1914. Ramanujan reached Cambridge on April 18, 1914.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 14pt; line-height: 150%;\">All in Cambridge were in awe of Ramanujan . He was awarded the B.A. degree in March 1916 for his work on \u2018Highly composite Numbers\u2019 which was published as a paper in the Journal of the London Mathematical Society. He was the second Indian to become a Fellow of the Royal Society in 1918 ( the first went to Adershir Cursetjee whose father was a Mumbai partner of <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>opium drug runners Rothschild , and who built the Cutty Sark with teak ). </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 14pt; line-height: 150%;\">Ramanujan became one of the youngest Fellows in the entire history of the Royal Society. He was elected \u201cfor his investigation in Elliptic Functions and the Theory of Numbers.\u201d On 13 October 1918 he was the first Indian to be elected a Fellow of Trinity College, Cambridge.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 14pt; line-height: 150%;\">Many bad things happened to Ramanujan in Cambridge, including his work getting stolen. Being a simpleton and a gentleman he kept quiet. Just like Nikola Tesla he would keep the proofs in his head. He did NOT make any notebook jottings while he was in England. Whatever he work was published , that was it. He published 21 papers there, five of which had Hardy\u2019s name as partner . </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">It took a while for him to catch on.&nbsp; His British sponsors would take a solved theorem from him, and pass it on to some Jew in Poland. Then it would be quickly translated to Polish, and the next week, Ramanujam would be asked \" Have you heard of a Polish Mathematician by the name of so and so-- because he has done the same work, last year!\"</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 14pt; line-height: 150%;\">The whole world knows about the LOST NOTE BOOK OF RAMANUJAN . This lost work included detailed work on Vedic sciences of <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Fractals, predictive modelling of String Theory, worm holes, Golden ratios, faster than light interstellar travel, Mandalas of microcosm and macrocosm like the Fractal Sri Yantra.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 14pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span>Ramanujan\u2019s deep understanding of Cosmic Consciousness, Fractal connectivity of the Cosmos , fractal collective sub conscious , Akashic memories, Portals, Fractal effect on Gravity for the Theory of everything -TOE, , <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>were reflected in his lost work. </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://1.gvt0.com/vi/RE2Lu65XxTU/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/RE2Lu65XxTU&fs=1&source=uds\" />\n<param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" />\n<embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/RE2Lu65XxTU&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br />\nIn the video above , they discuss Fibonacci series and Golden ratio-- all this was<span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\"> stolen by Fibonacci</span> from 2600 year old Vedic texts, translated ino Arabic from Bejaya, Algeria&nbsp;. Even a letter took 2 months to reach.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br />\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 14pt; line-height: 150%;\">Even honourable Nikola Tesla did not make allegations , though he knew the role of Rothschild agent JP Morgan and those who burned down his lab and how Edison and Marconi stole his work.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 14pt; line-height: 150%;\">It is rumoured that the military was behind this lost book, and that Ramanujan was poisoned. All peer reviewed magazines did propaganda that Ramanujan was made of weak stock, and that he had lost couple of brothers and sisters at childbirth.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 14pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span>One thing was sure, he suffered acutely from malnutrition. , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 14pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"background-color: white;\">Ramanujan developed an approximate formula in 1918, which helped him spot that numbers ending in 4 or 9 have a partition number divisible by 5, and he found similar rules for partition numbers divisible by 7 and 11.<br />\n<br />\nHe offered no proof but said that these numbers had \"simple properties\" possessed by no others.</span></span><br />\n<span lang=\"EN\" style=\"background: yellow; In 1943 after Tesla's death,&nbsp;the US court reversed the decision and proclaimed that Nikola Tesla is the inventor or radio and NOT Marconi. Being a Serb and a Orthodox church member, Tesla was subject to racism too.<br />\n<br />\nBut even Nikola Tesla and the whole of the Western world and the Nobel committee themselves knew that Marconi stole from Sir JC Bose, an Indian-- a genius far ahead of his time.<br />\n<br />\nAs early as 1896, JC Bose demonstrated the radio in front of the British Governor General. You must know that during this time India were slaves of the British Crown. He transmitted in front of the Governor General and a select audience more than 3 miles. This distance was from Presidency College Calcutta to Science College Calcutta.<br />\n<br />\nAt this time Swami Vivekananda advised him along with many of his admirers that he must Patent his work. He did NOT understand why knowledge should be patented and hence ignored this advise.<br />\n<br />\nIn 1896 Bose had travelled to London for a lecture tour and naively gave lot of information to Marconi- he never expected this man to steal his intellectual rights.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-WNwdpGw-wEM/TrWJ87MGJLI/AAAAAAAAHuI/D8lu9g592nE/s1600/RRR.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"282\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-WNwdpGw-wEM/TrWJ87MGJLI/AAAAAAAAHuI/D8lu9g592nE/s400/RRR.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nIn 1899 JC Bose travelled to London and again demonstrated his work in front of a huge scientific committee, in the Royal Society of London. The audience&nbsp;included Lord Rayleigh ,( the Nobel Prize winner of Physics in 1904), JA Fleming , Professor of London University who leaked the secrets to Marconi, and Lord Lister President of Royal Society, among other eminent scientists. <br />\n<br />\nHe was immediately offered Professorship of Cambridge which Bose refused on the spot, pissing off the powers that be. <br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Dou56oD_afc/TrWJ3qlUQ7I/AAAAAAAAHuA/UQRs3xEZako/s1600/RRR.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"254\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Dou56oD_afc/TrWJ3qlUQ7I/AAAAAAAAHuA/UQRs3xEZako/s320/RRR.png\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nMany people had seen Marconi in the audience too. He was in London when Bose lost his research papers from his hotel room, including the circuit diagrams.<br />\n<br />\nLater it was found that Marconi used exactly the same circuit diagram ( Coherer with telephone detector ) invented by Bose. Thief Marconi could NOT explain how this circuit works. <br />\n<br />\nHe then gave the lame excuse that a Italian Naval Engineer Solari developed it. Solari when asked to explain , refused point blank and said that he has nothing to do with it.&nbsp; Marconi then insisted that Italian professor Timasina drew the circuits, which Timasina again could NOT explain properly. The next man liar Marconi had in line in line was Paolo Castellini , who could also not explain how the circuit works. <br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red; font-size: x-large;\"><strong>What a disgrace!</strong></span><br />\n<br />\nJC Bose did NOT want to visit USA and he never did so. A single blow given in blind rage will&nbsp;be 100% lethal-- and I usually walk away from situations where fools dare me to do my worst. <br />\n<br />\nI am reminded of an similar incident which happened in my life at the age of 27 - today I am 55.&nbsp; I was a Ship Captain , NOT yet married .&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\nBeing a Captain means that I don't need any lecture on social responsibility . This happened in a&nbsp;cinema theatre next to Mumbai Gateway of India ( guess it is Regal ) for the 7 PM show.&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\nI was alone .<br />\n<br />\nThe Dress Circle section where I sat was chock a block , as the movie was a hit. In those days they would play some documentaries before the main movie started. <br />\n<br />\nIn front of me 6 seats were empty. Pretty soon 3 girls and 3 boys ( around 18 to 20 years old ) trooped in, &nbsp;and sat in front of me.<br />\n<br />\nFrom their dress code and their English speaking accent I knew they were the typical Bandra party--short frocks ,&nbsp;bob hair cuts, signature French beards , cross chains, and Bandra slang. One of them had long dreadlocks like what our&nbsp;man Rueben Fernandes, used to sport before.<br />\n<br />\nSuddenly a Mahatma Gandhi black and white documentary started. <br />\n<br />\nNow Gandhiji is a soul who commands extreme respect in India. <br />\n<br />\nIn my previous blog about VAIKOM MUHAMMAD BASHEER I has mentioned that as a boy Basheer just touched Gandhiji's hand and became a revolutionary. <br />\n<br />\nGandhiji was hence my hero - like for 99% of Indians. Lakshmi, the Mother of the Worlds, who dwells on the chest of Vishnu, the enemy of the demons, Madhu and Kaitabha), of attractive and divine form, with the nature of granting what is desired by those seeking refuge!<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"center\" style=\"line-height: 115%; text-align: center;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue;\"><em><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">tava suprabhatam aravindalochane!</span><br />\n<span class=\"slokatext1\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">bhavatu prasannamukha-chandramandale! </span></span><br />\n<span class=\"slokatext1\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">vidhisankarendra-vanitabhir archite! vrsasailanatha-dayite!dayanidhe</span></span></em><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"center\" style=\"line-height: 115%; text-align: center;\">\nMay it be an auspicious dawn to Thee, O! Lakshmi, the beloved of the Lord of Vrsacala, with eyes like lotus petals, with a bright face like the Moon, who is worshipped by Vani, Girija and Pulomaja (the wives of Brahma, Sankara and Indra) and who is very compassionate<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"center\" style=\"line-height: 115%; text-align: center;\">\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">atryadi-saptarsayas samupasya sandhyam </span><br />\n<span class=\"slokatext1\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">aksasindhu-kamalani manoharani, </span></span><br />\n<span class=\"slokatext1\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">adaya padayugam archayitum prapanna sesadri-sekhara-vibho! tava suprabhatam</span></span>.</span> </em><o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"center\" class=\"normaltext\" style=\"line-height: 115%; margin: 1em 0in; text-align: center;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Having worshipped the morning twilight and said their morning prayers, called <em>sandhyavandana</em>, the seven sages like Atri, bringing the beautiful lotuses from the divine Ganges, have arrived to worship Thy feet. Lord of Seshachala! May it be an auspicious dawn to Thee<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"center\" style=\"line-height: 115%; text-align: center;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue;\"><em><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">panchananabjabhava sanmukha vasavadyah traivikramadi charitam vibudhah stuvanti, </span><br />\n<span class=\"slokatext1\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">bhasapatith pathati vasarasuddhim arat </span></span><br />\n<span class=\"slokatext1\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">sesadri-sekhara-vibho! tava suprabhatam</span></span></em>.</span> <o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"center\" style=\"line-height: 115%; text-align: center;\">\nThe Gods, like the five-headed Brahma, the lotus-born Subrahmanya, and the six-headed Indra are praising the deeds of your incarnations as the Trivikramavatara. Nearby is Brhaspati who is reading out the planetary position (called Panchangam) of the day. Lord of Seshachala! May it be an auspicious dawn to Thee. <o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"center\" style=\"line-height: 115%; text-align: center;\">\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\"><span class=\"slokatext1\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">isatpraphulla-sarasiruha-narikela- pugadrumadi-sumanohara-palikanam avati mandam anilah saha divyagandhaih sesadri-sekhara-vibho! tava suprabhatam</span></span><o:p></o:p></span></em></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"center\" class=\"normaltext\" style=\"line-height: 115%; margin: 1em 0in; text-align: center;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">The breeze, carrying the wonderful fragrance of the partly-opened lotuses, and the beautiful trees like the Areca and Coconut, is blowing gently. Lord of Seshachala! May it be an auspicious dawn to Thee.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"center\" style=\"line-height: 115%; text-align: center;\">\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">unmilya netrayugam uttama-panjarastah</span><br />\n<span class=\"slokatext1\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">patravasista-kadaliphalapayasani,</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"slokatext1\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">bhuktva salilam atha kelisukhah pathanti</span></span><br />\n</span><span class=\"slokatext1\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">sesadri-sekara-vibho! tava suprabhatam.</span> </span></span></em><o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"center\" class=\"normaltext\" style=\"line-height: 115%; margin: 1em 0in; text-align: center;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">The parrots in their cages are opening their eyes, and graciously singing, after eating the remains of the plantain fruits and the <em>payasam</em> in the vessels. The ocean of nectar of compassion and other virtues! The chief of the Gods! The sole refuge of the Universe! The possessor of Sri (wealth)! One whose feet are worshipped by Ananta and Garuda! Lord of Venkatachala! May it be an auspicious dawn to Thee.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"center\" style=\"line-height: 115%; text-align: center;\">\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">sripadmanabha! purusottama! vasudeva!</span><br />\n<span class=\"slokatext1\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">vaikuntha! madhava! janardana! chakrapane! </span></span><br />\n<span class=\"slokatext1\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">srivasta-chihna! sarangata-parijata! </span></span><br />\n<span class=\"slokatext1\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">sri-venkatachalapate! tava suprabhatam.</span></span></span></em><o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"center\" class=\"normaltext\" style=\"line-height: 115%; margin: 1em 0in; text-align: center;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Padmanabha! Purushottama! Vasudeva! Vaikunta! Madhava! Janardana! Chakrapani! Bearer of the mole Srivatsa! Celestial tree (<em>parijata</em>) under whom refuge is sought! Lord of Venkatachala! May it be an auspicious dawn to Thee. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"center\" style=\"line-height: 115%; text-align: center;\">\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">kandarpa-darpa-hara-sundara-divyamurte! </span><br />\n</span><span class=\"slokatext1\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">kanta-kucamburuha-kutmala-loladrste! kalyana-nirmala-gunakara! divyakirte! sri-venkatachalapate! tava suprabhatam</span> </span></span></em><o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"center\" class=\"normaltext\" style=\"line-height: 115%; margin: 1em 0in; text-align: center;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Bearer of the charming and divine form surpassing the pride of Cupid (Manmatha)! One whose sight is fondly centred on the lotus bud like breasts of His beloved! The abode of auspicious and pure virtues! The possessor of Divine fame! Lord of Venkatachala! May it be an auspicious dawn to Thee. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<i><span style=\"color: #b31e1a; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">minakrte!kamatha!kola!nrsimha!varnin! svamin!parasvatha-tapodhana!ramachandra! <br />\nsesamsarama! yadunandana! kalkirupa! <br />\nsri-venkatachalapate! tava suprabhatam</span></span></i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"> <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"center\" style=\"line-height: 115%; text-align: center;\">\nLord in ten incarnations of Matsya (Fish), Kamatha (Tortoise), Kola (Boar), Narasimha (Man-lion) Trivikrama (Dwarf), Parasurama, Rama, Balarama, Krishna and Kalki! Lord of Venkatachala! May it be an auspicious dawn to Thee. </div>\n<div align=\"center\" style=\"line-height: 115%; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div align=\"center\" style=\"line-height: 115%; text-align: center;\">\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\"><span class=\"slokatext1\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">ela-lavanga-ghanasara-sugandhi-tirtham divyam viyat-sariti hema-ghatesu purnam, dhrtvadya vaidika-sikhamanayah prahrstah tisthanti venkatapate tava suprabhatam. </span></span><o:p></o:p></span></em></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"center\" class=\"normaltext\" style=\"line-height: 115%; margin: 1em 0in; text-align: center;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">The Brahmins, well-versed in the Vedas, are now joyfully waiting to worship you. They are carrying golden pots on their heads that are filled with the water of the Divine Ganges (Akasa Ganga), which has been rendered fragrant by mixing cardamom, cloves and camphor in it. Lord of Venkatachala! May it be an auspicious dawn to Thee. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"center\" style=\"line-height: 115%; text-align: center;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue;\"><em><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">bhasvan udeti vikachani saroruhani sampurayanti ninadaih kakubho vihangah,</span><br />\n<span class=\"slokatext1\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">srivaisnavas satatam arthita-mangalas te dhamasrayanti tava venkata! suprabhatam. </span></span></em><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"center\" class=\"normaltext\" style=\"line-height: 115%; margin: 1em 0in; text-align: center;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">The Sun is rising; the lotuses have blossomed; the birds are twittering; the Sri Vaishnavas, always imploring auspiciousness, are waiting at Thy abode. Lord of Venkatachala! May it be an auspicious dawn to Thee.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"center\" class=\"slokatext\" style=\"line-height: 115%; margin: 1em 0in; text-align: center;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"><em><span style=\"color: #b31e1a;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">brahmadayas suravaras samaharsayas te santas sanadana-mukhastv atha yogivaryah,<br />\ndhamantike tava hi mangala-vastu-hastah <br />\nsri-venkatachalapate! tava suprabhatam.</span> <o:p></o:p></span></em></span></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"center\" class=\"normaltext\" style=\"line-height: 115%; margin: 1em 0in; text-align: center;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Brahma,the great sages and the good Yogins as Sanandana are waiting at Thy abode, with auspicious offerings in their hands. Lord of Venkatachala! May it be an auspicious dawn to Thee<b>. </b><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"center\" style=\"line-height: 115%; text-align: center;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue;\"><em><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">laksminivasa! niravadya-gunaika-sindho! samsara-sagara-samuttaranaika-seto!</span><br />\n<span class=\"slokatext1\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">vedantu-vedya-nijavaibhava! bhaktabhogya! </span></span><br />\n<span class=\"slokatext1\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">sri-venkatachalapate! tava suprabhatam. </span></span></em><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div align=\"center\" style=\"line-height: 115%; text-align: center;\">\n<span class=\"normaltext1\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\">Abode of Lakshmi! Ocean of faultless and auspicious virtues! Bridge to cross the ocean of transmigration (samsara)! One whose glory is known through the Upanishads! One who is enjoyed by devotees! Lord of Venkatachala! font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><em><span style=\"color: red;\">As per legend the gentle strains of this Stotra rouses up Lord Vishnu from His slumber every morning.&nbsp;</span></em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: #1a3052; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><em><span style=\"color: red;\">An early morning recitation of the Venkatesha Suprabhatam&nbsp;creates keenness in purpose for the rest of the day.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: #1a3052; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><em><span style=\"color: red;\">This is the reason why Shri Venkatesha Stotra is an excellent way to start the day and organize the mind and body. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Chanting this Stotra or listening closely to it imparts all these benefits.</span></em>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; All dead were Indians except 6 British nationals.</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-7rNcjL4zF-g/TrGKiIJg21I/AAAAAAAAHqo/7g7mfTR_zM4/s1600/imagesCA2DZAUM.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Just 13 days before Indian PrimeMinister Lal Bahadur Shastri died of a mysterious heart attack while at Tashkent, after a pact with Pakistan to end the 1965 Indo-Pak war.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Surprisingly ( NOT so surprisingly for some ) India did NOT make any attempts to do an investigation, considering that Homi Bhabha was a very valuable Indian.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Daniel Roche, a French&nbsp;enthusiast spent 5 years collecting the pulverised parts of the aircraft Kanchenjunga over a 25 square kilometer area.&nbsp; He collected three tonnes of it around Mont Blanc , the highest peak of the Alps, including the black box and personal jewellery.. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">According to him, (and also to a layman with commonsense), such wide scattering is possible only by a <span style=\"color: red; font-size: x-large;\">missile strike by a military fighter jet.</span>&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">If it was a plane crash or a collision, there wold have been a fire considering there was 42000 litres of Jet fuel on board in the fuel tanks.</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Roche was ready to give it to the Govt of India-- all he wanted was India to pay for the shipment charges. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; Both Kakrapar-1 and -2 units are loaded with 500kg of thorium fuel to improve their operation at start-up.&nbsp;&nbsp;</em></span><br />\n<span style=\"color: #333333; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><em><br /></em></span>\n<span style=\"color: #333333; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><em>In 1995, Kakrapar-1 achieved about 300 days of full power operation and Kakrapar-2 about 100 days using thorium fuel. A 30kW mini-reactor has successfully operated at India's Kamini reactor at Kalpakkam.&nbsp; And the use of thorium-based fuel is planned in Kaiga-1 and -2 and Rajasthan-3 and -4 (Rawatbhata) reactors.&nbsp;</em></span><br />\n<span style=\"color: #333333; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><em><br /></em></span>\n<span style=\"color: #333333; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><em>India has a three-stage plan for nuclear energy.&nbsp; Stage one uses uranium-fuelled PHWRs (pressurised heavy water reactors) and LWRs to produce plutonium.&nbsp; In stage two this plutonium-based fuel is used in FBRs to breed U-233, and more plutonium and thorium.&nbsp;</em></span><br />\n<span style=\"color: #333333; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><em><br /></em></span>\n<span style=\"color: #333333; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><em>Stage three uses advanced heavy water reactors to burn the U-233 and Pu-239 with thorium.&nbsp;
